[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer detected a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte write operation that overflows a stack-allocated[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvariable [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`tmp371`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m by writing at offset [0m[1;36m120[0m[39m of an [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte buffer allocated at [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moffset [0m[1;36m112[0m[39m.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is a **stack-buffer-overflow** vulnerability with a SCARINESS score of [0m[1;36m46[0m[39m, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclassified as a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte-write-stack-buffer-overflow. The vulnerability involves [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwriting beyond the boundaries of a stack-allocated buffer, which can lead to memory[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorruption, crashes, or potential code execution depending on exploitation [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcircumstances.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Issue Details[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe overflow occurs during the following sequence of operations:[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The fuzzer invokes `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` with test input from `[0m[35m/[0m[95mtestcase[0m[39m`[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. This triggers `mg_http_parse` to process HTTP data[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. During parsing, `mg_log` is called to log information[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. The logging function uses `mg_vxprintf` for formatted output[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. When formatting a double value via `mg_dtoa`, the code path leads to [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`mg_snprintf` and `mg_vsnprintf`[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Eventually, `mg_vxprintf` calls `scpy` which invokes `mg_putchar_iobuf_static`[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. The actual overflow occurs in `mg_pfn_iobuf_private` at address `[0m[1;36m0x7f741d56fb78[0m[39m`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Stack Frame Analysis[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAccording to the AddressSanitizer report, the overflow occurs in the `mg_vxprintf` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction's stack frame at `[0m[35m/src/mongoose/src/[0m[95mfmt.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m247[0m[39m`. The frame contains two [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mobjects:[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `tmp` at offset [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m32[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m72[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m40[0m[39m bytes[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `tmp371` at offset [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m112[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m120[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m bytes[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe memory access at offset [0m[1;36m120[0m[39m overflows the `tmp371` variable by [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m byte, writing [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimmediately after the allocated [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte buffer.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Code Path Investigation[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe call stack reveals the vulnerability path through multiple formatting and [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moutput functions:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Primary Path:**[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `mg_http_parse` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mhttp.[0m[1;92mc:317[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m → Entry point from HTTP parsing[0m                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability is a **stack-buffer-overflow** in the `%e`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`%E` format specifier [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhandler within `src/fmt.c`. The issue stems from a buffer size mismatch:[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Line [0m[1;36m318[0m[39m**: Allocates an [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte stack buffer: `char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;`[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Line [0m[1;36m322[0m[39m**: Requests up to [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m bytes from `mg_dtoa`: `[0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, mantissa,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m8[0m[39m, c == [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWhen `mg_dtoa` internally calls `[0m[1;35mmg_snprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdst, dstlen, [0m[32m"%s"[0m[39m, buf[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` at line [0m[1;36m204[0m[39m, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mit creates an `mg_iobuf` structure with `[0m[33msize[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m10[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe `dstlen` parameter[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHowever, the actual buffer `tmp` only has [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m bytes. When `mg_pfn_iobuf_private` [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwrites characters and checks `io->len + [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m <= io->size`, it uses `io->[0m[33msize[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m10[0m[39m` for [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mboundary checking, causing writes at offsets [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m and [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m to overflow the [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte buffer.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Comprehensive Fix Strategy[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Primary Fix [0m[1;39m([0m[39msrc/fmt.c lines [0m[1;36m318[0m[39m and [0m[1;36m322[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:**[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m**: Modify line [0m[1;36m318[0m[39m to increase the buffer size from [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m to [0m[1;36m40[0m[39m bytes:[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Change from:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchar tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m To:[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchar tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m40[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m**: Modify line [0m[1;36m322[0m[39m to use `[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` instead of the hardcoded value [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;36m10[0m[39m`:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Change from:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mk = [0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, mantissa, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, c == [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m To:[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mk = [0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, mantissa, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, c == [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why this is the optimal approach:**[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Alignment with existing patterns**: The codebase already uses `char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m40[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand `[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` for the `%g`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`%f` format specifiers at lines [0m[1;36m275[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m280[0m[39m. This fix [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbrings the `%e`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`%E` handler in line with the established safe pattern.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Buffer reuse consideration**: The `tmp` buffer is reused at line [0m[1;36m326[0m[39m for [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mmg_lld[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, exponent, [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, which can write up to [0m[1;36m21[0m[39m bytes for a [0m[1;36m64[0m[39m-bit integer.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe [0m[1;36m40[0m[39m-byte buffer accommodates both:[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Mantissa conversion [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvariable length with decimal points[0m[1;39m)[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Exponent conversion [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmax ~[0m[1;36m21[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Safety margin**: The [0m[1;36m40[0m[39m-byte size matches `mg_dtoa`'s internal buffer size [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m139[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, ensuring adequate space for any realistic double-to-string conversion [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mincluding scientific notation.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Minimal code change**: Only two lines need modification, reducing the risk of [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintroducing new bugs.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **No functional changes**: The fix only corrects the buffer size; the formatting[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic remains unchanged.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**How it preserves existing codebase logic:**[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The format specifier behavior [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`%e`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`%E`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains identical[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The mantissa/exponent calculation logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m319[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m321[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m324[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m327[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is untouched[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Other format specifiers are unaffected[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The `mg_dtoa` and `mg_lld` function calls remain the same, just with a larger [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdestination buffer[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The `scpy` operations [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m323[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m327[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m continue to work correctly, now with [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39madequate buffer space[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**How it addresses the evaluation report:**[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Eliminates the overflow**: The [0m[1;36m40[0m[39m-byte buffer with `[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` ensures the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer size matches the capacity passed to `mg_dtoa`[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Fixes the root cause**: Addresses the fundamental mismatch between allocated [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m8[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and requested capacity [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m10[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Handles the trigger path**: The HTTP parsing error that logs with `%e` format [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mhttp.[0m[1;92mc:316[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will no longer cause overflow[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Maintains deterministic behavior**: The fix ensures consistent, safe operation [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor all double values[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential side effects and mitigation:**[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Stack usage increase**: The fix increases stack usage by [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m bytes [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfrom [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m to [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m40[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m per invocation of the `%e`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`%E` handler. [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: This is negligible for modern systems and matches existing [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstack usage for `%g`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`%f` handlers. The mongoose library is designed for embedded [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msystems that can accommodate [0m[1;36m40[0m[39m-byte stack allocations.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **No ABI changes**: This is an internal fix to a static buffer; no API or ABI [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchanges occur.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **No performance impact**: The buffer size increase has no measurable [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mperformance impact on formatting operations.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Reference to similar solutions:**[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix directly mirrors the proven safe implementation for `%g`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`%f` format [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecifiers at lines [0m[1;36m275[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m280[0m[39m:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchar tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m40[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [33m...[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mk = [0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, v, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m pr, c == [0m[32m'g'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis demonstrates that the [0m[1;36m40[0m[39m-byte buffer with `[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` pattern is the [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mestablished, tested approach in this codebase for double-to-string formatting.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Implementation Steps[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Open `src/mongoose/src/fmt.c`[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Locate line [0m[1;36m318[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwithin the `else if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc == [0m[32m'e'[0m[39m || c == [0m[32m'E'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` block[0m[1;39m)[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Change `char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;` to `char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m40[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;`[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Locate line [0m[1;36m322[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe `mg_dtoa` call within the same block[0m[1;39m)[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Change `[0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, mantissa, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, c == [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to `[0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmantissa, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, c == [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Verify the changes compile without errors[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Test with the provided fuzzer testcase to confirm the overflow is resolved[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Verification[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter applying the patch:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Run the fuzzer with the original testcase to verify no AddressSanitizer errors[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Test various edge cases: very large numbers [0m[1;39m([0m[39m>[0m[1;36m10[0m[39m^[0m[1;36m21[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, very small numbers [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m<[0m[1;36m10[0m[39m^[0m[1;36m-21[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, infinity, NaN[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Confirm `%e` and `%E` format specifiers produce correct output in logging [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctions[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Run existing test suites to ensure no regression[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Verify with AddressSanitizer that no memory errors occur during normal operation[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    int64_t exponent = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint64_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35mlog10[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mmy_fabs[0m[1;39m([0m[39md[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    double mantissa = d [0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;35mpower[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, exponent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    k = [0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, mantissa, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, c == [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Changed [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m to [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    n += [0m[1;35mscpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout, param, tmp, k[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mout[0m[1;39m([0m[39mc, param[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    n++;[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    k = [0m[1;35mmg_lld[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, exponent, [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    n += [0m[1;35mscpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout, param, tmp, k[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Why This Is the Optimal Approach[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Follows Established Pattern**: Looking at lines [0m[1;36m272[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m280[0m[39m, the [0m[32m'g'[0m[39m and [0m[32m'f'[0m[39m format [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecifiers use identical logic:[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Declare `char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m40[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m275[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Call `[0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, v, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m pr, c == [0m[32m'g'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m280[0m[1;39m)[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis pattern has been proven safe and correct for similar floating-point formatting[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperations.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Proper Sizing**: [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `mg_dtoa` internally uses a [0m[1;36m40[0m[39m-byte buffer [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m139[0m[39m: `char buf[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m40[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;`[0m[1;39m)[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `mg_lld` can output up to [0m[1;36m20[0m[39m bytes for extreme int64_t values [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m19[0m[39m digits + sign[0m[1;39m)[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A [0m[1;36m40[0m[39m-byte buffer safely accommodates both operations[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Eliminates Size Mismatch**: Using `[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` ensures the actual buffer size [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand the size parameter passed to `mg_dtoa` always match, even if the buffer size is[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchanged in the future.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. How It Preserves Existing Logic[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**No Algorithm Changes**: The fix only modifies buffer sizing, not the scientific [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnotation algorithm or output format.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**No API Changes**: The function signature and behavior remain identical from the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcaller's perspective.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**No Functional Changes**: The output format for [0m[32m'e'[0m[39m and [0m[32m'E'[0m[39m specifiers remains [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munchanged - only the internal buffer handling is made safe.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Maintains Buffer Reuse**: The buffer is still reused for both mantissa and [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexponent conversion, maintaining the efficiency of the original design.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. How It Addresses the Issues[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Fixes the Overflow**: [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Current: [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte buffer with [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m-byte writes → [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m-byte overflow[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Fixed: [0m[1;36m40[0m[39m-byte buffer with [0m[1;36m40[0m[39m-byte capacity → no overflow[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Addresses All Three Bugs**:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. ✅ Insufficient buffer: [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m → [0m[1;36m40[0m[39m bytes[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. ✅ Size mismatch: hardcoded [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m → [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m = [0m[1;36m40[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. ✅ Buffer reuse safety: [0m[1;36m40[0m[39m bytes accommodates both mg_dtoa and mg_lld[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Handles Edge Cases**:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Large mantissa values that produce long string representations[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Extreme exponents [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthough double exponents are typically [0m[1;36m-308[0m[39m to +[0m[1;36m308[0m[1;39m)[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Special values like infinity and NaN [0m[1;39m([0m[39mhandled by mg_dtoa[0m[1;39m)[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Overflow Mechanism Explained[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe overflow occurs through this call chain:[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Line [0m[1;36m322[0m[39m: `[0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, mantissa, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, c == [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Actual buffer: [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m bytes[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Told buffer: [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m bytes ❌[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. `mg_dtoa` → `[0m[1;35mmg_snprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdst, [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, [0m[32m"%s"[0m[39m, buf[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfmt.[0m[1;92mc:204[0m[1;39m)[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Creates iobuf with [0m[33msize[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m10[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. `mg_vsnprintf` → `mg_vxprintf` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mprintf.[0m[1;92mc:47[0m[1;39m)[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Writes characters through output function[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. `mg_putchar_iobuf_static` → `mg_pfn_iobuf_private` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mprintf.[0m[1;92mc:37[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m38[0m[1;39m)[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Checks: `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mio->len + [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m <= io->size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` where [0m[33msize[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m10[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Writes up to [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m bytes[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Overflow occurs**: Bytes [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m and [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m write beyond the [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte `tmp` buffer[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix ensures buffer size [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m40[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ≥ dstlen parameter [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m40[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, preventing overflow.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effect**: Increased stack usage by [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m bytes per call[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Mitigation**: [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Acceptable: `mg_vxprintf` is not recursively called to great depth[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Consistent: Matches stack usage of [0m[32m'g'[0m[39m and [0m[32m'f'[0m[39m format specifiers[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Typical stack frames are much larger [0m[1;39m([0m[39moften kilobytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, so [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m bytes is negligible[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**No other side effects**: [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No performance impact [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstack allocation is fast[0m[1;39m)[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No compatibility issues [0m[1;39m([0m[39moutput format unchanged[0m[1;39m)[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No breaking changes to existing tests[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m. Similar Solutions in Codebase[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix directly mirrors the existing implementation at lines [0m[1;36m272[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m280[0m[39m:[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Lines [0m[1;36m272[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m280[0m[39m: CORRECT pattern for [0m[32m'g'[0m[39m and [0m[32m'f'[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc == [0m[32m'd'[0m[39m || c == [0m[32m'u'[0m[39m || c == [0m[32m'x'[0m[39m || c == [0m[32m'X'[0m[39m || c == [0m[32m'p'[0m[39m ||[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    c == [0m[32m'g'[0m[39m || c == [0m[32m'f'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  bool s = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc == [0m[32m'd'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, h = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc == [0m[32m'x'[0m[39m || c == [0m[32m'X'[0m[39m || c == [0m[32m'p'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m40[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m ✅ [0m[1;36m40[0m[39m bytes[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  size_t xl = x ? [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m : [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc == [0m[32m'g'[0m[39m || c == [0m[32m'f'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    double v = [0m[1;35mva_arg[0m[1;39m([0m[39m*ap, double[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpr == ~0U[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m pr = [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    k = [0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, v, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m pr, c == [0m[32m'g'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m ✅ [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe [0m[32m'e'[0m[35m/[0m[32m'E'[0m[39m handler should follow this exact same pattern since it also calls [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`mg_dtoa` for floating-point conversion.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Conclusion[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix is minimal, safe, and follows established patterns in the codebase. It [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maddresses all three identified bugs and completely eliminates the [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstack-buffer-overflow vulnerability without any negative side effects or breaking [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchanges.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis Summary[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter analyzing the evaluation report and code snippets, I've confirmed the root [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcause of the persistent stack-buffer-overflow:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe issue occurs in the [0m[32m'e'[0m[35m/[0m[32m'E'[0m[39m format specifier handler in `mg_vxprintf`. There [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mare **two critical bugs**:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Buffer size mismatch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mPRIMARY[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: Line [0m[1;36m318[0m[39m/[0m[1;36m820[0m[39m allocates `char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` but [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mline [0m[1;36m322[0m[39m/[0m[1;36m824[0m[39m passes size `[0m[1;36m10[0m[39m` to `[0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. This causes `mg_dtoa` to call [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mmg_snprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdst, [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, [0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, which creates an `mg_iobuf` with [0m[33msize[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, allowing [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwrites beyond the actual [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte buffer.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Insufficient buffer size [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSECONDARY[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: Even with correct size parameters, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbytes is too small. The buffer is reused for both mantissa [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvia `mg_dtoa`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexponent [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvia `mg_lld`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Large exponents can require up to [0m[1;36m21[0m[39m bytes [0m[1;39m([0m[39msign + [0m[1;36m19[0m[39m [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdigits[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why Previous Patch Failed[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe previous patch modified `src/fmt.c` but **the build system compiles [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`mongoose.c` instead**. The codebase has both:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `src/fmt.c` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m317[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m327[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - individual source file[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `mongoose.c` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m819[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m829[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - amalgamated file with identical buggy code[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe buggy code in `mongoose.c` remained unpatched, causing the persistent overflow [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith identical ASAN characteristics.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Call Chain Verification[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe overflow is triggered by:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. `mg_http_parse` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m316[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m → `MG_ERROR` macro → `mg_log` → `mg_vxprintf`[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Format string contains `%e` for scientific notation of `message.len`[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. `mg_vxprintf` processes [0m[32m'e'[0m[39m handler → `mg_dtoa` → `mg_snprintf` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mrecursive[0m[1;39m)[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. `mg_pfn_iobuf_private` writes at tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39moffset [0m[1;36m120[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m overflowing [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte buffer[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Comprehensive Fix Strategy[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Files to Patch[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mApply identical fixes to **BOTH** files:[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **src/fmt.c** at lines [0m[1;36m318[0m[39m and [0m[1;36m322[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **mongoose.c** at lines [0m[1;36m820[0m[39m and [0m[1;36m824[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Required Changes[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFor each location, make two changes:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Change [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m**: Increase buffer size[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **src/fmt.c line [0m[1;36m318[0m[39m**: `char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;` → `char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m40[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;`[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **mongoose.c line [0m[1;36m820[0m[39m**: `char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;` → `char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m40[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;`[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Change [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m**: Pass correct buffer size to mg_dtoa[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **src/fmt.c line [0m[1;36m322[0m[39m**: `[0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, mantissa, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, c == [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` → `[0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, mantissa, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, c == [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **mongoose.c line [0m[1;36m824[0m[39m**: `[0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, mantissa, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, c == [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` → [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, mantissa, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, c == [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Justification[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why this is the optimal approach:**[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Matches existing patterns**: The fix follows the proven pattern used for [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m'g'[0m[35m/[0m[32m'f'[0m[39m format handlers [0m[1;39m([0m[39msrc/fmt.c lines [0m[1;36m275[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m280[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Uses `char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m40[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;` for buffer allocation[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Uses `[0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` for correct size passing[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Sufficient buffer size**: [0m[1;36m40[0m[39m bytes safely accommodates:[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `mg_dtoa` output: up to ~[0m[1;36m30[0m[39m characters for mantissa with maximum precision[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `mg_lld` output: up to [0m[1;36m21[0m[39m characters for INT64_MIN exponents [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[1;36m-9223372036854775808[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Safe buffer reuse for both mantissa and exponent operations[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Preserves existing logic**: [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes to algorithm or format output behavior[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Scientific notation format remains: mantissa + [0m[32m'e'[0m[35m/[0m[32m'E'[0m[39m + exponent[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All existing tests in `test/unit_test.c` remain valid [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexpects [0m[32m"3.33e0"[0m[39m, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"3.33e12"[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Eliminates ASAN error**: [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Fixes buffer size mismatch [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m10[0m[39m vs [0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that caused write at offset [0m[1;36m120[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Prevents overflow from large exponent formatting[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Handles edge cases [0m[1;39m([0m[39mspecial values, extreme doubles[0m[1;39m)[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Addresses both files**: By patching both `src/fmt.c` and `mongoose.c`, the fix[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mworks regardless of which file the build system uses[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential side effects and mitigation:**[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Stack usage increase**: +[0m[1;36m32[0m[39m bytes per [0m[32m'e'[0m[35m/[0m[32m'E'[0m[39m format invocation[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: Acceptable overhead, consistent with [0m[32m'g'[0m[35m/[0m[32m'f'[0m[39m handlers, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnegligible impact[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Build system compatibility**: Patching both files ensures fix applies [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mregardless of build configuration[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: No conflicts since changes are identical[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Edge cases**: Now properly handles:[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Special values [0m[1;39m([0m[39minf, nan, [0m[1;36m0.0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m via mg_dtoa's early returns[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Large exponents [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlog10 of DBL_MAX/DBL_MIN[0m[1;39m)[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Recursive mg_snprintf calls with correct buffer sizes[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why previous approaches failed:**[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Only patched `src/fmt.c`, but build uses `mongoose.c`[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This fix patches both files to ensure complete coverage[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
